  11: - New column: cancel_requested (INTEGER 0/1).
  12: - request_cancel: queued → cancelled atomically (T1, instant); in_progress
  13:   → set the cancel flag (T2, cooperative — the worker observes it).
  14: - mark_in_progress is now a compare-and-swap (only transitions a queued,
  15:   not-cancel-requested row) so a queued cancel cannot be overwritten.
  16: - is_cancel_requested / mark_cancelled support the worker's cooperative
  17:   abort path.
  18: 
  19: Default DB path: state/v6_runs.sqlite (gitignored). Override via env
  20: `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB`. WAL mode enabled.
  21: """
  22: 
  23: from __future__ import annotations
  24: 
  25: import json
  26: import os
  27: import sqlite3
  28: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  29: from typing import Any
  30: 
  31: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  32: 
  33: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
  34: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
  35: 
  36: # Lifecycle states from which a run can no longer transition. Public so the
  37: # /runs/{id}/cancel endpoint shares one definition of "terminal".
  38: TERMINAL_STATUSES = ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")
  39: 
  40: # Columns selected by get_run (single source of truth for both the
  41: # first-attempt and post-migration-retry queries).
  42: _RUN_COLUMNS = (
  43:     "run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
  44:     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
  45:     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id, "
  46:     "cancel_requested"
  47: )
  48: 
  49: 
  50: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
  51:     if path is not None:
  52:         return path
  53:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
  54: 
  55: 
  56: def _now_iso() -> str:
  57:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
  58: 
  59: 
  60: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  61:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  62:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  63:     if parent:
  64:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  65:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  66:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  67:     return conn
  68: 
  69: 
  70: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  71:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  72: 
  73:     1. Create base table if absent.
  74:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  75:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  76:        SQLite 3.34+).
  77:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a / I-rdy-011 field if missing.
  78:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  79:     """
  80:     conn.execute(
  81:         """
  82:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
  83:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  84:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
  85:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
  86:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
  87:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
  88:             started_at TEXT,
  89:             finished_at TEXT,
  90:             result_json TEXT,
  91:             error_json TEXT
  92:         )
  93:         """
  94:     )
  95:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
  96:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
  97:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
  98:         cols.discard("status")
  99:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
 100:     for col_name, col_type in {
 101:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
 102:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
 103:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
 104:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
 105:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
 106:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
 107:         "cancel_requested": "INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0",
 108:     }.items():
 109:         if col_name not in cols:
 110:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
 111:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
 112:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
 113: 
 114: 
 115: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
 116:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent."""
 117:     conn = _connect(path)
 118:     try:
 119:         conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
 120:         _migrate_schema(conn)
 121:         conn.commit()
 122:     finally:
 123:         conn.close()
 124: 
 125: 
 126: def insert_run(run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 127:     """Insert a new row with lifecycle_status='queued'. Raises IntegrityError on duplicate."""
 128:     init_db(path)
 129:     conn = _connect(path)
 130:     try:
 131:         conn.execute(
 132:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
 133:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
 134:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
 135:         )
 136:         conn.commit()
 137:     finally:
 138:         conn.close()
 139: 
 140: 
 141: def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 142:     """Transition queued → in_progress IFF the run is not cancel-requested.
 143: 
 144:     I-rdy-011: compare-and-swap. The `WHERE lifecycle_status='queued' AND
 145:     cancel_requested=0` guard means a queued cancel that already flipped the
 146:     row to 'cancelled' cannot be overwritten by a worker picking the run up.
 147: 
 148:     Returns True iff the row transitioned; False means the run was cancelled
 149:     (or already past 'queued') and the caller must not run the pipeline.
 150:     """
 151:     conn = _connect(path)
 152:     try:
 153:         cur = conn.execute(
 154:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? "
 155:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued' AND cancel_requested=0",
 156:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 157:         )
 158:         conn.commit()
 159:         return cur.rowcount > 0
 160:     finally:
 161:         conn.close()
 162: 
 163: 
 164: def request_cancel(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> str | None:
 165:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011).
 166: 
 167:     - queued run → atomically transitioned to terminal 'cancelled' (T1,
 168:       instant — the worker's mark_in_progress CAS will then no-op).
 169:     - in_progress run → cancel_requested flag set; lifecycle stays
 170:       'in_progress' until the worker observes the flag at a pipeline stage
 171:       boundary and calls mark_cancelled (T2, cooperative).
 172: 
 173:     Returns the resulting lifecycle_status ('cancelled' or 'in_progress'),
 174:     or None if the run does not exist or is already terminal.
 175:     """
 176:     conn = _connect(path)
 177:     try:
 178:         # T1: queued → cancelled, atomically.
 179:         cur = conn.execute(
 180:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 181:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued'",
 182:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 183:         )
 184:         if cur.rowcount > 0:
 185:             conn.commit()
 186:             return "cancelled"
 187:         # T2: in_progress → set the flag for the worker to observe.
 188:         cur = conn.execute(
 189:             "UPDATE runs SET cancel_requested=1 "
 190:             "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='in_progress'",
 191:             (run_id,),
 192:         )
 193:         conn.commit()
 194:         return "in_progress" if cur.rowcount > 0 else None
 195:     finally:
 196:         conn.close()
 197: 
 198: 
 199: def is_cancel_requested(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
 200:     """True iff a cancellation has been requested for the run.
 201: 
 202:     Best-effort: a missing run / missing table returns False.
 203:     """
 204:     conn = _connect(path)
 205:     try:
 206:         try:
 207:             row = conn.execute(
 208:                 "SELECT cancel_requested FROM runs WHERE run_id=?", (run_id,)
 209:             ).fetchone()
 210:         except sqlite3.OperationalError:
 211:             return False
 212:         return bool(row["cancel_requested"]) if row is not None else False
 213:     finally:
 214:         conn.close()
 215: 
 216: 
 217: def mark_cancelled(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 218:     """Terminal transition → lifecycle_status='cancelled' + finished_at.
 219: 
 220:     Used by the worker when it observes cancel_requested at a pipeline
 221:     stage boundary (cooperative T2 abort), and as the actor's mapping for a
 222:     pipeline-A manifest with status 'cancelled'.
 223:     """
 224:     conn = _connect(path)
 225:     try:
 226:         conn.execute(
 227:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
 228:             "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
 229:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
 230:         )
 231:         conn.commit()
 232:     finally:
 233:         conn.close()

 236: def set_pipeline_meta(
 237:     run_id: str,
 238:     *,
 239:     query_slug: str | None = None,
 240:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None,
 241:     artifact_dir: str | None = None,
 242:     decision_id: str | None = None,
 243:     path: str | None = None,
 244: ) -> None:
 245:     """Set pipeline-A metadata after the actor learns the slug/dir.
 246: 
 247:     Independent of lifecycle transition so the actor can record meta as
 248:     soon as pipeline-A starts, before the run completes.
 249:     """
 250:     conn = _connect(path)
 251:     try:
 252:         conn.execute(
 253:             "UPDATE runs SET query_slug=COALESCE(?, query_slug), "
 254:             "manifest_run_id=COALESCE(?, manifest_run_id), "
 255:             "artifact_dir=COALESCE(?, artifact_dir), "
 256:             "decision_id=COALESCE(?, decision_id) WHERE run_id=?",
 257:             (query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, decision_id, run_id),
 258:         )
 259:         conn.commit()
 260:     finally:
 261:         conn.close()

 264: def mark_completed(

 285: def mark_aborted(

 293:     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
 294:

 297:     """

 299:     try:
 300:         conn.execute(

 307:                 cost_usd,
 308:                 run_id,
 309:             ),
 310:         )
 311:         conn.commit()
 312:     finally:
 313:         conn.close()

 316: def mark_failed(run_id: str, error: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
 317:     """Operational failure (exception, missing manifest, unknown status, etc).

 356: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 357:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 358: 
 359:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 360:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 361:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 362:     contract.
 363: 
 364:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 365:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 366:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 367:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 368:     """
 369:     conn = _connect(path)
 370:     try:
 371:         try:
 372:             row = conn.execute(
 373:                 f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 374:                 (run_id,),
 375:             ).fetchone()
 376:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 377:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 378:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 379:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 380:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 381:             # missing-row.
 382:             if "no such table" in msg:
 383:                 return None
 384:             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
 385:             if "no such column" in msg:
 386:                 conn.close()
 387:                 init_db(path)
 388:                 conn = _connect(path)
 389:                 row = conn.execute(
 390:                     f"SELECT {_RUN_COLUMNS} FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 391:                     (run_id,),
 392:                 ).fetchone()
 393:             else:
 394:                 raise
 395:     finally:
 396:         conn.close()
 397:     if row is None:
 398:         return None
 399:     return _row_to_response(row)

 151: # Grace period (seconds) after run_store reports lifecycle_status terminal but
 152: # no Redis terminal event has been seen. After this elapses, emit a synthetic
 153: # `run_complete(status=stream_lost)` so the client gets a deterministic close
 154: # rather than hanging on keepalives forever. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3 + diff iter-1.
 155: STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS = 10.0

 157: 
 158: def _get_lifecycle_status(external_run_id: str) -> str | None:
 159:     """Best-effort sync run_store lookup. Returns lifecycle_status or None.
 160: 
 161:     Imported lazily so tests that don't touch run_store don't pay sqlite init.
 162:     Any failure (missing DB, import error, schema drift) returns None so the
 163:     reader keeps emitting keepalives rather than synthesizing a stream_lost
 164:     terminal on transient backend hiccups.
 165:     """
 166:     try:
 167:         from polaris_v6.queue import run_store  # noqa: PLC0415
 168: 
 169:         row = run_store.get_run(external_run_id)
 170:         if row is None:
 171:             return None
 172:         return getattr(row, "lifecycle_status", None)
 173:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — observability lookup never blocks SSE
 174:         logger.warning(
 175:             "[run_events] run_store lookup failed run_id=%s: %s",
 176:             external_run_id,
 177:             exc,
 178:         )
 179:         return None
 180: 
 181: 
 182: async def _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id: str) -> bool:
 183:     """Async wrapper for the sync sqlite lookup."""
 184:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 185:     status = await asyncio.to_thread(_get_lifecycle_status, external_run_id)
 186:     # I-rdy-011 (#507): `cancelled` is terminal — a queued-cancel writes no
 187:     # Redis terminal event, so without this an SSE consumer would hang on
 188:     # keepalives until the run is forgotten.
 189:     return status in ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")

 191: 
 192: def _is_connection_failure(exc: BaseException) -> bool:
 193:     """Narrow stream_unavailable to actual Redis reachability failures.
 194: 
 195:     Per Codex diff iter-1 P1: every XREAD exception was being mapped to
 196:     stream_unavailable, masking schema bugs / corrupt entries as 'Redis down'.
 197:     Now we treat ONLY connection/timeout/socket failures as unavailability;
 198:     other exceptions surface as stream_lost.
 199:     """
 200:     if isinstance(exc, (ConnectionError, TimeoutError, OSError)):
 201:         return True
 202:     # redis.asyncio raises ConnectionError subclasses; check by class name
 203:     # to avoid a hard import dependency.
 204:     name = type(exc).__name__
 205:     return name in {
 206:         "ConnectionError",
 207:         "TimeoutError",
 208:         "BusyLoadingError",
 209:         "ConnectionResetError",
 210:         "RedisConnectionError",
 211:     }

 214: async def read_events(
 215:     external_run_id: str,
 216:     last_event_id: str = "0-0",
 217:     *,
 218:     block_ms: int = 5000,
 219:     redis_client_async=None,
 220: ) -> AsyncIterator[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]:
 221:     """Async generator yielding (stream_id, raw_pipeline_event_dict).
 222: 
 223:     Terminates after emitting a `run.completed` event. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3
 224:     + diff iter-1 P1:
 225: 
 226:     - empty XREAD window → keepalive (caller emits SSE comment frame), then
 227:       check run_store. While lifecycle_status is queued/in_progress, keep
 228:       emitting keepalives.
 229:     - lifecycle_status in {completed, failed} AND no terminal event seen in
 230:       the next STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS → emit a synthetic
 231:       run_complete(status=stream_lost) and close cleanly.
 232:     - actual Redis connection/timeout failure → emit
 233:       run_complete(status=stream_unavailable) and close.
 234:     - non-reachability XREAD exception → emit stream_lost and close (treat as
 235:       degraded stream rather than 'Redis down').
 236:     """
 237:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 238: 
 239:     last_id = _validate_last_event_id(last_event_id)
 240:     key = EVENT_STREAM_KEY.format(run_id=external_run_id)
 241: 
 242:     try:
 243:         if redis_client_async is None:
 244:             import redis.asyncio as aredis  # noqa: PLC0415
 245:             client = aredis.from_url(_redis_url(), decode_responses=False)
 246:         else:
 247:             client = redis_client_async
 248:     except ImportError:
 249:         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 250:         return
 251: 
 252:     # Tracks first-seen-at for lifecycle_status terminal so we can apply the
 253:     # grace window before declaring stream_lost.
 254:     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen: float | None = None
 255:     loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
 256: 
 257:     try:
 258:         while True:
 259:             try:
 260:                 events = await client.xread({key: last_id}, count=100, block=block_ms)
 261:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
 262:                 if _is_connection_failure(exc):
 263:                     logger.warning(
 264:                         "[run_events] redis unreachable run_id=%s: %s",
 265:                         external_run_id,
 266:                         exc,
 267:                     )
 268:                     yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 269:                     return
 270:                 # Non-reachability failure — log and degrade to stream_lost.
 271:                 logger.warning(
 272:                     "[run_events] xread error run_id=%s: %s",
 273:                     external_run_id,
 274:                     exc,
 275:                 )
 276:                 yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 277:                 return
 278: 
 279:             if not events:
 280:                 # Empty XREAD window — emit keepalive then consult run_store.
 281:                 yield ("__keepalive__", {})
 282:                 if await _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id):
 283:                     now = loop.time()
 284:                     if lifecycle_terminal_first_seen is None:
 285:                         lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = now
 286:                     elif now - lifecycle_terminal_first_seen >= STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS:
 287:                         logger.warning(
 288:                             "[run_events] lifecycle terminal without redis terminal "
 289:                             "run_id=%s — emitting synthetic stream_lost",
 290:                             external_run_id,
 291:                         )
 292:                         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 293:                         return
 294:                 else:
 295:                     # Reset the grace window if the run un-terminals (shouldn't happen,
 296:                     # but the lifecycle is the source of truth).
 297:                     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = None
 298:                 continue
 299: 
 300:             # Real events arrived → reset the grace window.

  58: def _derive_slug(template_id: str, question: str) -> str:
  59:     """Deterministic URL-safe slug for pipeline-A run_dir nesting.
  60: 
  61:     Pipeline-A reads q['slug']; this produces a stable, human-readable
  62:     identifier per (template, question) pair. UUID provides uniqueness
  63:     via the artifact_dir parent — slug itself doesn't need to be unique.
  64:     """
  65:     base = f"{template_id}_{question[:60]}"
  66:     cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", base.lower()).strip("_")
  67:     return cleaned[:120] or "untitled"

1112: def _abort_if_cancelled(

1115:     run_id: str,
1116:     summary: dict,
1117:     log_fn,
1118: ) -> bool:

1120: 
1121:     If a cancellation was requested for this v6 run, write a terminal
1122:     `cancelled` manifest, emit the SSE terminal event, mark the summary, and
1123:     return True so run_one_query aborts early at this stage boundary. Returns
1124:     False for non-v6 runs or when no cancel is pending.

1127:     never aborted on a transient backend hiccup.
1128:     """

1134: 
1135:         if not run_store.is_cancel_requested(ext):
1136:             return False
1137:     except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — cancel-check failure must not abort a healthy run
1138:         return False

1140:     manifest = {

1142:         "slug": q.get("slug", ""),
1143:         "domain": q.get("domain", ""),
1144:         "question": q.get("question", ""),
1145:         "status": "cancelled",

1149:     )
1150:     emit_event(ext, "run.completed", {"status": "cancelled"})
1151:     summary["status"] = "cancelled"
1152:     return True

   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
   8: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
   9: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  10: no-op.
  11: """

  14:

  17:

  19:

  21: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  22: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest

  24: 
  25: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  26: 
  27: 
  28: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  29: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  30:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  31:     try:
  32:         run_store.insert_run(run_id, payload.template, payload.question)
  33:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  34:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  35:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  36:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  37:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  38:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
  39: 
  40:     enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, payload.model_dump())
  41: 
  42:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  43:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
  44:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
  45:     return record
  46: 
  47: 
  48: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
  49: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
  50:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  51:     if record is None:
  52:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
  53:     return record
  54: 
  55: 
  56: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
  57: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
  58:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
  59: 
  60:     - Unknown run → 404.
  61:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
  62:       returns the current record (200).
  63:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
  64:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
  65:     """
  66:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  67:     if record is None:
  68:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
  69:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
  70:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
  71: 
  72:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
  73: 
  74:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  75:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago
  76:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after cancel")
  77:     return updated

   1: """Run-status response schema.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12): split lifecycle (operational) from pipeline_status
   4: (pipeline-A manifest verdict). Old `status` retained as computed alias for
   5: tests/v6/ backcompat — populated from lifecycle_status.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (2026-05-16): `cancel_requested` surfaced so the UI can show a
   8: cancel as in-flight in <5s, before an in-progress run reaches the next
   9: pipeline stage boundary and transitions to terminal `cancelled`.
  10: """

  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, computed_field
  17: 
  18: LifecycleStatus = Literal[
  19:     "queued",
  20:     "in_progress",
  21:     "completed",
  22:     "cancelled",
  23:     "failed",
  24: ]
  25: 
  26: PipelineStatus = Literal[
  27:     "success",

  33:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  34:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  35:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  36:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  37:     "abort_no_sources",
  38:     "abort_evaluator_critical",
  39:     "error_unexpected",
  40: ]
  41: 
  42: # Backcompat alias used by older code/tests (tests/v6/ asserts body['status']
  43: # and record.status). Computed from lifecycle_status by the model.
  44: RunStatus = LifecycleStatus
  45: 
  46: 
  47: class RunStatusResponse(BaseModel):
  48:     run_id: str = Field(..., description="Server-assigned UUID hex.")
  49:     lifecycle_status: LifecycleStatus = Field(
  50:         ...,
  51:         description="Operational lifecycle: queued → in_progress → completed|failed|cancelled.",
  52:     )

"""Tests for queue.actors — research-run actor stubs.

Verifies the Phase 0 actor surface:
  - enqueue_research_run echoes payload + reports completed status
  - enqueue_research_run carries max_retries=3 + 30-min time_limit
  - cancel_research_run records cancel_requested intent
  - cancel_research_run uses max_retries=0 (cancel is fire-and-forget)
  - module-level ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES constant matches actor decoration

These tests pin the contract so the Phase 1 bridge wiring (when
adapters/retrieval_bridge.py replaces the noop) can't silently change
the public interface.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import pytest

pytest.importorskip("dramatiq")

# Session-shared StubBroker is installed by tests/v6/conftest.py so the
# @dramatiq.actor decorators in polaris_v6.queue.actors bind against the
# SAME broker that the acceptance suite uses. (Cycle-4 audit P1.1 fix.)
from polaris_v6.queue.actors import (  # noqa: E402
    ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES,
    cancel_research_run,
    enqueue_research_run,
)


def test_enqueue_returns_completed_status_and_echoes_payload():
    payload = {"question": "ozempic CV?", "template": "clinical"}
    result = enqueue_research_run.fn("run-001", payload)
    assert result == {
        "run_id": "run-001",
        "status": "completed",
        "echo": payload,
    }


def test_enqueue_handles_empty_payload():
    result = enqueue_research_run.fn("run-empty", {})
    assert result["run_id"] == "run-empty"
    assert result["status"] == "completed"
    assert result["echo"] == {}


def test_enqueue_max_retries_constant_is_3():
    assert ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES == 3


def test_enqueue_actor_carries_max_retries_3():
    """The @dramatiq.actor decoration must match the documented constant."""
    assert enqueue_research_run.options.get("max_retries") == 3


def test_enqueue_actor_time_limit_is_30_minutes_in_ms():
    """30 minutes = 1,800,000 ms — long enough for cluster runs."""
    assert enqueue_research_run.options.get("time_limit") == 30 * 60 * 1000


def test_cancel_returns_cancel_requested_status():
    result = cancel_research_run.fn("run-002")
    assert result == {"run_id": "run-002", "status": "cancel_requested"}


def test_cancel_actor_max_retries_is_0():
    """Cancel is fire-and-forget — never retry."""
    assert cancel_research_run.options.get("max_retries") == 0


def test_actors_are_dramatiq_actor_instances():
    """Both actors must be wrapped via the @dramatiq.actor decorator."""
    assert hasattr(enqueue_research_run, "send")  # actor.send() enqueues
    assert hasattr(enqueue_research_run, "fn")    # actor.fn is the unwrapped callable
    assert hasattr(cancel_research_run, "send")
    assert hasattr(cancel_research_run, "fn")
